## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5e1e-1413">Windows Server 2008 R2 屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e1e-1413">Windows Server 2008 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a5e1e-1414">此類別包含 Windows Server 2008 R2 的下列屬性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e1e-1414">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>
